      <div n="6" type="sthāna">
        <head>[Uttaratantra 31-66]</head>

        <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 31: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.1"><label>6.31.1</label> athāto revatīpratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.3"><label>6.31.3</label> aśvagandhā ja śṛṅgī ca śārivātha
            purnarnnavā |
            <caesura/>
             sahavidārī ca tathā kaṣāyaḥ pariṣecane | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.4"><label>6.31.4</label> tailam abhyaṅgane kāyaṃ kuṣṭhe
            sarjarase tathā |
            <caesura/>
             palaṃ kaṣāyainalade tathā girikadaṃbake | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.5"><label>6.31.5</label> vaṭāś ca
            karṇṇakakubhadhātakītindūkeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             kākolyādau gaṇecāpi pāṇīyaṃ sarpir iṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6cd"><label>6.31.6cd</label> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi tathā
            yavaphalāghṛtaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.7"><label>6.31.7</label> saṃdhyayor ubhayoḥ kāryam etad
            uddhūpanaṃ śiśā |
            <caesura/>
             varuṇāriṣṭakamayaṃ rumakaṃ saindhavaṃ tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.8"><label>6.31.8</label> dhāraye dyāpi satataṃ vacā
            putrakajīvake |
            <caesura/>
             śuklāḥ sumanaso lājapayaḥ śālyodanaṃ tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.9"><label>6.31.9</label> valin nivedya gotīrthe
            revatyaiprayatātmanā |
            <caesura/>
             saṃgame ca bhiṣak snānaṃ kuryād dhātrīkumārayoḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.10"><label>6.31.10</label> nānāvastradharādevī
            citramālyānulepanā |
            <caesura/>
             calatkuṇḍalinī śyāmā revatīte prasīdatu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.11"><label>6.31.11</label> yām upāsannisatataṃ devyo
            vividhabhūṣaṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             lamvākarālāvinatā tathaiva vahuputrikā |
            <caesura/>
             raivatī śuṣkanāsā ca sā ca devī prasīdatām iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || 3 || ❈ || </p>
        </div>


        <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 32: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.1"><label>6.32.1</label> athātaḥ pūtanāpratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.3"><label>6.32.3</label> kapotavaṃkāharalaḥ varuṇaḥ
            pāribhadrakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āsphotā caiva yojyāḥ syur vālasya pariṣecane | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.4"><label>6.32.4</label> vacā vayaḥ sthā golomī haritālaṃ
            manaḥ śilā |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhaṃ sarjarasaṃ caiva tailārthe vargam iṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.5"><label>6.32.5</label> hitaṃ ghṛtan tukākṣīryāḥ siddhaṃ
            madhurakeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣthatālīsakhadirāḥ rṣapajñane tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.6"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.7"><label>6.32.7</label> śaṇanākulakumbhīkā majjāno vadarasya
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             karkaṭāsthi ghṛtañ cāpi dhūpanaṃ saha sarṣapaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.8"><label>6.32.8</label> kākādanīñ citraphalāṃ vimvīṃ guñjāñ
            ca dhārayet |
            <caesura/>
             matsyodanañ ca kurvīta kṛśaram palalaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             śarāvasampuṭakṛtam valiṃ śūnyagṛhe haret | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.9ab"><label>6.32.9ab</label> utsṛṣṭān nābhiṣekaś ca śiśoḥ
            snapanam iṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.9cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.10"><label>6.32.10</label> malināmvarasamvītā
            malinārūkṣamūrdhajā |
            <caesura/>
             śūnyāgāśrayādevī dārakaṃ pātu pūtanā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.11"/>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || 3 || ❈ || </p>

        </div>
        <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 33: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.1"><label>6.33.1</label> athātāndhapūtanāpratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.3"><label>6.33.3</label> tiktakadrumāṇāṃ patraiś ca kvāthaḥ
            kāryo vasecane |
            <caesura/>
             surā sauvīrakañ kuṣṭhaṃ haritālam manaḥ śilā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.4"><label>6.33.4</label> tathā sarjarasaṃ cāpi tailārtham
            apasaṃharet ||
            <caesura/>
             pippalīpippalīmūlaṃ vargam madhurakam madhuḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.5ab"><label>6.33.5ab</label> sālaparṇī vṛhatyau ca ghṛtārtham
            api vuddhimāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.5cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.6"><label>6.33.6</label> purīśaṃ kaukkuṭaṃ keśāḥ ścarmma
            sarvppatvageṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             jīrṇṇāñ ca bhikṣusaṃghāṭīṃ dhūpanāyopakalpayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.7"><label>6.33.7</label> kukkuṭīṃ markaṭīvimvīm anantāś cāpi
            dhārayet ||
            <caesura/>
             māṃsamāmaṃ tathā pakvaśoṇitañ ca catuḥ pathe| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.8"><label>6.33.8</label> nivedyam antañ ca gṛhe śiśoḥ
            snapanam iṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.9"><label>6.33.9</label> karālapiṃgalā muṇḍā kaṣāyam
            varadhāriṇī |
            <caesura/>
             devī vālam imaṃ prītā rakṣatām andhapūtanā iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || || ❈ || </p>
        </div>


        <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 34: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.1"><label>6.34.1</label> athātaḥ śītapūtanāpratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.3"><label>6.34.3</label> viṃvīkāpitthaṃ sūrasaṃ tathā
            vilvapracīvalau |
            <caesura/>
             nandībhallātakañ cāpi pariṣeke vacārayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.4"><label>6.34.4</label> vastamūtraṃ gavaṃ mūtramūstañ
            cāmaradārū ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhañ ca sarvagandhañ ca tailārtham avacārayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.5"><label>6.34.5</label>
            rohiṇīsarjakhadirapalāśakakubhatvacaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             niḥkvāthya tasminniḥ kvāthe sakṣīraṃ vipaceddhṛtaṃ| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.6"><label>6.34.6</label> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi vastagandhāṃ
            sahāṃ vacāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nivasya patrāṇi tathā dhūpanārthaṃ prayojayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.7"><label>6.34.7</label> dhārayed api guñjāñ ca lamvāṃ
            kākādanīn tathā |
            <caesura/>
             nadhyāṃ mudgadanaiś cāpi tarpayec chītapūtanāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.8ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.8cd"><label>6.34.8cd</label> jalāyaśānte vālasya spanaṃñ
            copadiśyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.9"><label>6.34.9</label> mugdodanāśinī devī surāśoṇitapāyinī
            |
            <caesura/>
             jalāśayaratādevī pātu tvāṃ śītapūtanā iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || || 0 || </p>
        </div>
        <div n="35" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 35: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.1"><label>6.35.1</label> athāto muṇḍikāpratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.3"><label>6.35.3</label> kapitthavilvau
            tarkārīvaṃśagandharvahastaka |
            <caesura/>
             kuverākṣī ca yojyāni vālasya pariṣecane | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.4"><label>6.35.4</label> svarasair bhṛṅgavṛkṣāṇāṃ tathaiva
            hayagandhayā | tailaṃ vasāṃ ca saṃyojya paced abhyañjanaṃ śiśāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.5"><label>6.35.5</label> madhūlikā payasyā ca tugākṣīdyo
            gaṇau na ca |
            <caesura/>
             madhuraiḥ pañcamūlyāś ca kanīyasyā ghṛtam pacet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.6"><label>6.35.6</label> yavāḥ sarjarasaḥ kuṣṭhaṃ
            sarpiścoddhūpanahitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             dhārayed api jihvāś ca cāṣavaiḍālasatyajāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.7"><label>6.35.7</label> varṇakaṃ cūrṇakaṃ mālyamañjanām
            pārataṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             manaḥ śilāṃ copaharet goṣṭhamadhye valiṃ śuciḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.8ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.8cd"><label>6.35.8cd</label> mantrapūtābhir adbhiś ca
            tatraiva snapanam bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.9"><label>6.35.9</label> alaṃkṛtā rūpavatī subhagā kāmarūpiṇī
            |
            <caesura/>
             goṣṭhamadhyālayā devī pātu tvāṃ mukhamaṇḍikā iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || || 0 || </p>
        </div>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.1"><label>6.36.1</label> athāto naigameṣapratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.3"><label>6.36.3</label> vilvāgnimanthapūtīkāḥ kāśmaryāḥ
            pariṣecane |
            <caesura/>
             savījañ cāpi dhānyāmlam pariṣekapraśasyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.4"><label>6.36.4</label> priyaṅgu saralānantā
            śatapuṣpākuṭannaṭaiḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             pacet tailaṃ surātakradadhimastvāmlakāñjikaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.5"><label>6.36.5</label> pañcamūladvayakvāthaiḥ kṣīre
            madhurakeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             paced ghṛtañ ca matimāṃ kharjūryā mastakena ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.6ab"><label>6.36.6ab</label> vacā vayasthā ¦ ¦ ¦ ¦ sahitāṃ
            jaṭilāṃ cāpi dhārayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.6cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.7"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.8"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.9"><label>6.36.9</label> tilataṇḍulakaṃ mālyaṃ bhakṣāṃś ca
            vividhāni ca | kumārapitṛmeṣāya vṛkṣamūle nivedayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.10ab"><label>6.36.10ab</label> adhastān kṣīravṛkṣasya
            snapanañ copadiśyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.10cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.11"><label>6.36.11</label> ajānanañ calākṣibhrū kāmarūpī
            mahāyaśāḥ |

             vālaṃ vālapitā devo naigameṣo bhirakṣatām iti || </l>

        <div n="37" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 37: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.1"><label>6.37.1</label> athāto grahotpattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
            |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.2a"><label>6.37.2a</label> atha khalu van</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.3"><label>6.37.3</label> navaskandādayaḥ proktā vālānāṃ ya
            ime grahāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrīmanto divyavapuṣo nārīpuruṣavigrahāṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.4"><label>6.37.4</label> ete guhasya ra kṛttikomāgniśūlibhiḥ
            | sṛṣṭāḥ śaravanasthāsya rakṣitasatmatejasā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.5"><label>6.37.5</label> strīvigrahāgrahā ye tu nānārūpā
            mayeritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             devīnāṃ kṛttikānān te bhāgā rājasatāmatāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.6"><label>6.37.6</label> naigameṣas tu pārvatyāḥ sṛṣṭo
            meṣānano grahaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kumāradhāro devasya guhasyātmodbhavasya vai | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.7"><label>6.37.7</label> skandāpasmāraṃ sañjayaḥ
            sognināgnisamadyutiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saivaskandasakho nāmnā viśākha iti cocyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.8"><label>6.37.8</label> skandaḥ sṛṣṭo bhagavatā devena
            tripurāriṇā |
            <caesura/>
             vibharti cāparaṃ saṃjñaṃ kumāra iti saṃgrahaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.9"><label>6.37.9</label> vālalīlādharo yoyaṃ devo
            rudrāgnisambhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mithyā vāleṣu bhavavāṃ na khalveṣu pravarttate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.10"><label>6.37.10</label> kumāraskandasāmānyād atra kecid
            paṇḍitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gṛṇhātītya parijñānād vruvate dehacintakāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.11"><label>6.37.11</label> tato bhagavati skande
            devasenāpatau kṛte |
            <caesura/>
             upatasthur grahāsdyute dīptaśaktidharaṃ guhaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.12"><label>6.37.12</label> ūcuḥ prāñjalaś caivanaṃ vṛttin no
            vidhdhaatsviti |
            <caesura/>
             teṣām arthe tataḥ skandaḥ śivaṃ devam acodayat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.13"><label>6.37.13</label> tato grahāṃ tān uvāca bhagavāṃ
            bhaganetrahā |
            <caesura/>
             tairyagyonim mānuṣañ ca devañ ca tritayaṃ jagat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.14"><label>6.37.14</label> parasparopakāreṇa varttate
            dhāryate tathā |
            <caesura/>
             devamanuṣyāṃ prīṇanti tairyagyonin tathaiva ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.15"><label>6.37.15</label> yathākālaṃ pravarttanta uṣṇaṃ
            varṣahimādribhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ijyāvalinamaskārair japya homais tathaiva caḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.16"><label>6.37.16</label> samyak prayuktaiś ca naraiḥ
            prīṇayaṃty atu devatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhāgadheyā vibhaktāś ca śeṣaṃ kiñcin na vidyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.17"><label>6.37.17</label> tad yuṣmākaṃ śubhā vṛttiḥ pūjāsv
            eva bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             kuleṣu yeṣu nejyaṃte devatāpitaras tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.18"><label>6.37.18</label> vrāhmaṇāḥ sādhavo vāpi
            guravotithayas tathā
            <caesura/>
             nivṛtta śaucācāreṣu tathā klaśopajīviṣu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.19"><label>6.37.19</label> utsannabhikṣavaliṣu tathā
            bhinnagṛheṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             gṛheṣu yeṣu te vālām stān hiṃsaṃ dhvamaśaṅkitāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.20"><label>6.37.20</label> tatra vo vipulā vṛttiḥ pūjā caiva
            bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃ grahāḥ samutpannā vālā hiṃ santi cāpy ataḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.21"><label>6.37.21</label> grahopasṛṣṭā vālās tu
            duścikitsyatamāḥ smṛtāḥ |

             vaikalyam maraṇam cāpi dhruvaṃ skandagrahe nṛṇām iti || </l>

              <item corresp="#SS.6.38.7.1-n2"> The reading <foreign>karṇṇinī</foreign> is
                not supported by our MSS here. However, it is found in both the parallel
                verse of the vulgate (6.38.8ab) and at a later instance in the Nepalese
                MSS (see, e.g., verse 12 below). It is likely that the superscipt
                  "<foreign>r</foreign>" in the reading of KL 699

                  "<foreign>i</foreign>". </item>

        <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 39: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <note>[This adhyāya is currently a rough version based on MSS NAK 5-333 and 699,
            being edited (2023-10-04).]</note>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.1"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.1</label> athāto jvarapratiṣedhaṃ
            adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||<anchor n="SS.6.39.1-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.1" type="apparatus">
            <list type="note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.39.1-n1">In reading <foreign>-utpatti</foreign>, the
                scribe of H may have been influenced by the title
                  <foreign>grahotpatti</foreign> of the immediately preceding adhyāya in
                his manuscript (he omits the <foreign>yonivyāpat</foreign>
                adhyāya).</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3.1"><label>6.39.3.1</label> atha khalu vatsa suśruta </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.3</label> yenāmṛtam apāṃ madhyād
            uddhṛtaṃ pūrvvajanmani |
            <caesura/>
             yato 'maratvaṃ saṃprāptās tridaśās tridiveśvarāḥ ||<anchor n="SS.6.39.3-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.3" type="apparatus">
            <list type="note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.39.3-n1">Dalhaṇa (p. 671) reported Jejjaṭa's reading
                  <foreign>tridaśās tridaśeśvarāḥ</foreign>, which is a mixture of the
                readings of witnesses K and H.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.4"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.4</label> śiṣyās taṃ devam āsīnaṃ
            papracchuḥ suśrutādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇasyopadravāḥ proktā vraṇinām apy ataḥ paraṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.5"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.5</label> samāsato vyāsataś ca brūhi
            no bhiṣajām vara |
            <caesura/>
             upadraveṇa juṣṭasya vraṇaḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.6"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.6</label> upadravāś ca vraṇinaḥ
            kṛcchrasādhytamo mataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya śeṣadhātuparikṣayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.7</label> tasmād upadravāṃ kṛtsnān
            vadasva vadatām vara | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.8"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.8</label> teṣān tad vacanaṃ śrutvā
            prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             jvaram ādau pravakṣyāmi sa rogānīkarāṭ smṛtaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.9"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.9</label> rudrakopāgnisaṃbhūtaḥ
            sarvvabhūtapratāpanaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             tais tair nnāmabhir anyeṣāṃ sattvānām parikīrttyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.10"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.10</label> janmādau nidhane caiva
            bhavatīha na saṃśayaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarvvavikārāṇāṃ jvaro rājā prakīrttitaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.11"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.11</label> ṛte devamanuṣyebhyo nānyo
            viṣaha te tu taṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.12"/>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.13"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.13</label> svedāvarodhaḥ santāpaḥ
            sarvvāṅgagrahaṇam bhṛśaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.14"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.14</label> yugapad yatra roge tu
            jvara ity upadiśyate ||

             syāt saptamī bhaktasamudbhavā ca liṅgāni tāsāṃ śṛṇu sauṣadhāni ||</l>

             dhūmam pibet snaihikamapramattaḥ pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ ghṛtam eva cātra || </l>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.5"><label>6.55.5</label> kṣuttṛṣṇocchvāsanidrāṇām udāvartto
            bhaved iha |
            <caesura/>
             vyāhanyamānavegārtta udāvartto nirucyate |
            <caesura/>
             tasyābhidhāsye vyāsena lakṣaṇaṃ sacikitsitaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.6"><label>6.55.6</label> trayodaśavidhasyāsya bhinnasyetais
            tu kāraṇaiḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.7"><label>6.55.7</label> ādhmānaśūlo hṛdayo parodhaṃ
            śirorujaṃ śvāsam atīva hikkāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             kāsapratiśyāyagalagrahatvād valāsapittaprasarañ ca ghoraṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.8"><label>6.55.8</label> kuryād apāno bhihataḥ svamārge
            hanyāt purīśaṃ mukhataḥ kṣiped vā |
            <caesura/>
             āṭopaśūlau parivarttanañ ca saṃgaḥ purīśasya tathordhvavātaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.9"><label>6.55.9</label> purīśamāsyād api vā nireti
            purīśavege bhihite narasya |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrasya vege bhihate naras tu kṛcchreṇa mūtraṃ sravate lpam alpaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.10"><label>6.55.10</label> meḍhre gude
            vaṃkṣaṇabastimuṣkanābhipradeśeṣv atha mūrdhni cāpi |
            <caesura/>
             ānaddhabasteś ca bhavanti tīvrā rujaś ca śūlair iva tudyate ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.11"><label>6.55.11</label> manyāgalastambhaśirovikārāḥ |
            jṛmbhopaghātāt pavanātmikā syuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tathākṣināsāvadanāmayāś ca bhavanti tīvrāḥ saha karṇṇarogaiḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.12"><label>6.55.12</label> ānandajam vāpy atha śokajam vā
            netrodakaṃ prāptam amuñcato hi |
            <caesura/>
             śirogurutvaṃ nayanāmayāś ca bhavanti tīvrāḥ saha pīnasena<del rend="erased"
              >ḥ</del>
          </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.13"><label>6.55.13</label> bhavanti gāḍhaṃ kṣavathor vighātāc
            chirokṣināsāśravaṇeṣu rogāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhasya pūrṇṇatvam atīva todaḥ kukṣau tu vāyor ubhayoḥ pravṛttiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.14"><label>6.55.14</label> udgāravege bhihate bhavanti jantor
            vikārāḥ pavanaprasūtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             chardyābhighātena bhavec ca kuṣṭhaṃ yenaiva doṣeṇa vidagdham annaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.15"><label>6.55.15</label> mūtrāyaṇe pāyuni muṣkayoś ca śotho
            rujā mūtravinigrahaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             śukrāśmarī tatsravaṇaṃ bhaved vā te te vikārābhihate tu śukre | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.16"><label>6.55.16</label> tandrāṅgamardāvaruci śramaś ca
            kṣudhor vikārā kṛśatā ca dṛṣṭā |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhāsyaśoṣaḥ śravaṇāvarodhas tṛṣṇābhighātād dhṛdayavyathā ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.17"><label>6.55.17</label> śrāntasya niśvāsavinigraheṇa
            hṛdrogamohāv atha vāpi gulmaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jṛmbho 'ṅgamardo ṅgaśirotha jāḍyaṃ nidrābhighātād athavāpi tandrī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.18"><label>6.55.18</label> tṛṣṇārdditaṃ parikliṣṭaṃ kṣīṇaṃ
            śūlair abhidrutaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             śakṛdvamantaṃ matimān udāvarttinam utsṛjet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.19"><label>6.55.19</label> sarsveṣv eteṣu vidhivad
            udāvartteṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vāyoḥ kriyā vidhātavyā svamārgapratipattaye | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.20"><label>6.55.20</label> sāmānyataḥ pṛthaktvena kriyāṃ
            bhūyo nibodha me |
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpanaṃ mārutaje snigdhasvinnam viśeṣataḥ </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.21"><label>6.55.21</label> purīśaje tu karttavyo vidhir
            ānāhikas tu yaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sauvarcalāḍhyāṃ madirāṃ mūtre tv abhihate pibet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.22"><label>6.55.22</label> elām vāpy atha madyena kṣīravāriṃ
            pibeta vā |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.23"><label>6.55.23</label> rasam aśvapurīśasya gardabhasya
            pibeta vā |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.24"><label>6.55.24</label> bhadradāru ghaṇaṃ mūrvāṃ haridrāṃ

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>
             ervārubījaṃ toyena pibed vā lavaṇīkṛtaṃ | </l>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.29"><label>6.55.29</label> tīkṣṇāṃjanāvapīḍābhyāṃ

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.37"><label>6.55.37</label> vāyuḥ koṣṭhānugo rūkṣaiḥ

             bhavec chāntim vrajaty evam udāvarttas tu dāruṇaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.45"><label>6.55.45</label> devadārvyagnikau kuṣṭhaṃ śuṇṭhīṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.6.55.48"><label>6.55.48</label> vacām ativiṣam pāṭhāṃ yavakṣāraṃ

             viṣūcyalasakau tasmād bhavec cāpi viḍaṃbikā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.4"><label>6.56.4</label> sūcībhir i<del rend="erased"
              >ra</del>va gātrāṇi tudaṃ santiṣṭhate nilaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yasyām ajīrṇṇāt sā vaidyair viṣūcīti nirucyate | </l>

            śanalolupāḥ || </l>

            <caesura/>
             vaivarṇṇyakampau hṛdaye rujaś ca bhavanti tasyāṃ śirasaś ca bhedaḥ | </l>

             tasyālasakam ācaṣṭe tṛṣṇodgārau ca yasya tu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.9"><label>6.56.9</label> tuṣṭan tu bhukta.m kaphamārutābhyāṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.10"><label>6.56.10</label> yatrastham āmaṃ hi rujārttam eva

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.14"><label>6.56.14</label> pathyā vacā hiṃgu viḍaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.15"><label>6.56.15</label> kṣārāgadam vā lavaṇaṃ viḍam vā

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.18"><label>6.56.18</label> uṣṇābhir adbhir magadhodbhavānāṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.19"><label>6.56.19</label> cchāyāviśuṣkā guḍikā kṛtās tāḥ

            <caesura/>
             suvāmitaṃ sādhu virecitaṃ vā sulaṅghitam vā manujaṃ viditvā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.20"><label>6.56.20</label> peyādibhir dīpanapācanīyaiḥ

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.21"><label>6.56.21</label> pravarttamānaṃ na yathāstam etad

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.22"><label>6.56.22</label> āmāśaye śūlam atho gurutvaṃ

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.23"><label>6.56.23</label> śvāsaś ca pakvāśayaje bhavanti
            liṅgāni cātrālasakodbhavāni |
            <caesura/>
             āmodbhave vāntam upakrameta saṃsaktabhaktaṃ kramadīpanīyaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.24"><label>6.56.24</label> athetaraṃ yo na śakṛd vameta taṃ
            sādhayet svinnam imaiḥ prayogaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viṣūcikāyāṃ parikīrttitāni dravyāṇi vairecanikāni yāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.25"><label>6.56.25</label> saṃcūrṇṇya varttim vitared

            <caesura/>
             svinnasya pāyau viniveśya tāś ca cūrṇṇāni caiṣāṃ pradhamet tu nāḍyā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.26"><label>6.56.26</label> mūtreṇa vā sādhya yathāvidhāṇaṃ
            dravyāni yāny ūrdhvam adhaś ca yānti |
            <caesura/>
             kvāthena tenāśu nirūhayīta mātrārdhayuktena samākṣikeṇa | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.56.27"><label>6.56.27</label> tribhaṇḍipiṣṭaṃ lavaṇaprakuñcaṃ
            datvā viriktaṃ kramam ādiśec ca |
            <caesura/>
             eteṣv eva ca tailena sādhitena sukhāmbunā | prāptaṃ yadi na ca syād vā
            bhāgeṣv eṣv anuvāsanam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.3"><label>6.57.3</label> doṣaiḥ pṛthak
            trividhasokasamucchrayāc ca bhaktāyaneṣu hṛdi cāvatate pragāḍhaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nānne rucir bhavati taṃ bhiṣajo vikāraṃ bhaktopaghātam iha pañcavidhaṃ
            vadanti | | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.4"><label>6.57.4</label> hṛcchūlaśoṣavamathuḥ svarasaṃkṣayāc
            ca vātā<add/> sadāhamadatṛḍ vamane ca pittaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pittāt kaphena hṛdaye gurutāvilepaḥ śleṣmaprasekavamathuḥ śiraso rujañ ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.5"><label>6.57.5</label> sarvātmakaṃ trividhaliṃgam atho
            vadanti ||
            <caesura/>
             śokopaghātajam athānilalakṣaṇais tu |
            <caesura/>
             vātātmake virasam āsyam arocake tu pittena tiktakaṭukaṃ madhuraṃ kaphena | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.6"><label>6.57.6</label> sarvair upetam upadhārayasannipāte |
            dainyaṃ bhṛśam bhavati śokasamudbhave tu |
            <caesura/>
             vāṃtovacādir anile vidhivat pibec ca snehoṣṇatoyamadirānyatamena cūrṇṇaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.7"><label>6.57.7</label>
            kṛṣṇāviḍaṃgayavabhasmahareṇubhārgīrāsnailahiṃgulavaṇottamanāgarāṇāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pitte guḍāmbumadhurair vamanaṃ praśastaṃ lehaś ca
            saindhavasitāmadhusarpiriṣṭaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.8"><label>6.57.8</label> nimbāmbuccharditavataḥ kaphaje
            nupānaṃ rājadrumāmbu madhunā tu sadīpyakāḍhyaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇṇaṃ yad uktam atha vā tilaje tad eva sarvaiś ca sarvakṛtam evam
            upakrameta | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.9"><label>6.57.9</label>
            drākṣāpaṭolaviḍavetrakarīranimbamūrvābhayākṣabadarāgalakendravṛkṣāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bījaiḥ karañjanṛpavṛkṣabhavaiś ca piṣṭai lehaṃ pacet surabhimūtrayutaṃ
            yathāvat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.10"><label>6.57.10</label> mustāvacākaṭukarohiṇinirdahanyas
            tulyātha vāpi rajanābhayasaṃprayuktā |
            <caesura/>
             mūtre vike dviradamūtrayutāḥ paced vā pāṭhāsamām ativiṣāṃ rajanāñ ca mukhyāṃ
            | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.11"><label>6.57.11</label> maṇḍūkim arkam amṛtāṃ
            raśalāṃgalākhyāṃ mūtre paceta mahiṣasya vidhāṇavidvān |
            <caesura/>
             etān na santi caturo bhyasatas tu lehān gulmāruciś ca śikhisādahṛdāmayāś ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.12"><label>6.57.12</label> sātmyāsvadeśacaritāṃ vividhāṃś ca
            bhakṣyāṃ pānāni mūlaphalaṣāḍavarogayogāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             seved rasāṃś ca vividhāṃ vividhaiḥ prakārair bhuñjīta vāpi
            laghurūkṣamanaḥsukhāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.13"><label>6.57.13</label> āsthāpanaṃ vividham atra virecanañ
            ca kuryān mṛdūni śirasaś ca virecanāni |
            <caesura/>
             trīṇy ūṣaṇāni triphalāṃ rajanīdvayañ ca cūrṇṇīkṛtāni yavaśūkavimiśritāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.14"><label>6.57.14</label> kṣaudrāyutāni vitaren
            mukhadhāvanārthaṃm anyāni tiktakaṭukāni ca bheṣajāni |
            <caesura/>
             mustādirājaphalavargadaśāṃgasiddhaḥ kvāthair jayen madhuyutair vividhaiś ca
            lehaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.15"><label>6.57.15</label> mūtrāsavair guḍakṛtaiś ca tathāpy
            ariṣṭaiḥ kṣārāsavaiś ca madhumādhavatulyagandhaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             syād eṣa eva kaphavātaharo vidhiś ca | śātiṃ gate hutabhuji praśamāya tasya | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.16"><label>6.57.16</label> icchāvināśabhayajeṣu ca bādhakeṣu
            | bhāvād bhavāya vitaret khalu śalyatāpān |
            <caesura/>
             artheṣu cātipatiteṣu punarbhavāya paurāṇikaśrutimukhair avamānayeta iti ||
            kāyaci || 20 || 0 || </l>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>
             srotobhir bastim āgamya mūtraṃ vyāpādayed atha | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2.ii"><label>6.58.2.ii</label> vivarṇṇam āvilaṃ sāṃdraṃ

            <caesura/>
             tato vegapratīghātād udāvarttena vāyunā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.3"><label>6.58.3</label> prapīḍyaśoṣyamāne tu mūtrarogās

            <caesura/>
             vātakuṇḍalikāṣṭhīlā vātabastis tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrātītaḥ sajaṭharo mūtrotsaṅgaḥ | || kṣayas tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.4"><label>6.58.4</label> mūtragranthir mūtraśukro mūtravātas
            tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>

            vastau savedanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtram āvadhyaviguṇo bhramaty ākuṇḍalīkṛtaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.6"><label>6.58.6</label> mūtram alpālpam atha vā sarujaṃ
            saṃpravarttate ||
            <caesura/>
             vātakuṇḍalikāṃ taṃ tu vyādhim vidyāt sudāruṇaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.7"><label>6.58.7</label> śakṛnmārgasya basteś ca vāyur
            antaram āśritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             aṣṭhīlāvadghanaṃ granthiṃ karoty acalam unnataṃ | </l>

            ca jāyate |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.9"><label>6.58.9</label> vegaṃ vidhārayed yas tu mūtrasya
            kuśalo naraḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.10"><label>6.58.10</label> mūtrasaṅgo bhavet tena
            bastikukṣinipīḍanaḥ |
            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>
             tasya nābhyeti yadi vā kathaṃ cit saṃpravarttate | </l>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.14"><label>6.58.14</label> nābher adhastād ādhmānaṃ janayet
            tīvravedanaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ mūtrajaṭharam vidyād adho bastinirodhaṇaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.15"><label>6.58.15</label> bastau vāpy atha nāle maṇau vā
            yasya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.1"><label>6.59.1</label> athāto mūtrāghātapratiṣedhaṃ
                <expan>vyā<ex>vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</ex></expan> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.2"><label>6.59.2</label> yadā mūtrayato jantoḥ mūtravego
            vihanyate |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrāghātaṃ vadanty etam aṣṭadhā sa tu vakṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.3"><label>6.59.3</label> vātena pittena kaphena sarvais
            tathābhighātaiḥ śakṛdaśmaribhyāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tathāparaḥ śarkarayā sukaṣṭo mūtropaghātaḥ paṭhito ṣṭamas tu<del
              rend="crossed out">ḥ</del> | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.4"><label>6.59.4</label> alpam alpaṃ bhṛśaṃpīḍya
            muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ
            <caesura/>
             saṃtudyamānaḥ kṛcchreṇa vātāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.5"><label>6.59.5</label> pītam vāpy atha vā raktaṃ
            muṣkamehanabastibhir
            <caesura/>
             agnineva ca dahṛmbhiḥ pittāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.6"><label>6.59.6</label> samunnaddhodaraḥ kṛcchrān
            muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃhṛṣṭaromā gurubhiḥ śleṣmāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.7"><label>6.59.7</label> dāhaśītarujāviṣṭo nānāvarṇṇam muhur
            muhus
            <caesura/>
             tāmyamānaḥ sa kṛcchreṇa sannipātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.8"><label>6.59.8</label> mūtravāhiṣu śalyena kṣateṣv
            abhihateṣu vā |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsu mūtrāghātas tu jāyate bhṛṣadāruṇaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.9"><label>6.59.9</label> vātāghātena liṅgāni tasya tulyāni
            nirddiśet ||
            <caesura/>
             śakṛtas tu pratīghātād vāyur viguṇatāṃ gataḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.10"><label>6.59.10</label> sādhmānañ ca samūlañ ca
            mūtrasaṅgaṃ karoti ca ||
            <caesura/>
             aśmarīsambhavasyoktaṃ mūtraghātasya lakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.11"><label>6.59.11</label> aśmarī śarkarā caiva śṛṇu
            kīrttayato mamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāyā viśeṣan tu śṛṇu kīrttayato mama | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.12"><label>6.59.12</label> pacyamānaṃ tu pittena śoṣyamānan
            tu vāyunā |
            <caesura/>
             śleṣmaṇā veṣṭitaṃ cūrṇṇaṃ śarkarety abhisañjñitaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13"><label>6.59.13</label> hṛtpīḍā vepathuḥ śūlaḥ kukṣāv
            agniś ca durbalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tābhir bhavati mūrcchā ca mūtrāghātaś ca dāruṇaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13i"><label>6.59.13i</label> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi
            mūtrāghātacikitsitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             kāryaṃ bhaved yathā yac ca śṛṇu kīrttayato mama ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13ii"><label>6.59.13ii</label> kaṣāyāny tha kalkāś ca lehāḥ
            svedās tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             hitā syur mūtraghāteṣu tathaivottarabastayaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13iii"><label>6.59.13iii</label> ervvārubījakalkaḥ syāc
            chlakṣṇapiṣṭaukṣasammitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhānyāmlbapeyo lavaṇo mūtrāghātena pīḍitaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13iv"><label>6.59.13iv</label> surāṃ sauvarcalavatīm
            pradhānāṃ prapiben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jīrṇṇabhuktaḥ sadā bhuñjaṃ saguḍaṃ śāntim arcchati |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13v"><label>6.59.13v</label> madhūdakena saṃloḍya karṣaṃ
            kuṃkumakasya vā |
            <caesura/>
             rātrau paryuṣitam pūtaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13vi"><label>6.59.13vi</label> dāḍimāṃmblayutaṃ madyaṃ
            śuṇṭhījīrakasaṃyutaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pītvā surāṃ salavaṇāṃ mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13vii"><label>6.59.13vii</label> pṛthakparṇyādivargañ ca
            svadaṃṣṭrāñ caiva tatsamaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             ardhaprasthena dugdhasya paced ardhāḍhakodake |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13viii"><label>6.59.13viii</label> kṣīrāvaśiṣṭam āhṛtya pūtaṃ
            sarpir vidhūpitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             śītīkṛtaṃ pibed enaṃ mūtrakṛcchraharan naraḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13ix"><label>6.59.13ix</label> gardasya śakṛd vāpi vājināṃ vā
            gavāṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             rasasya tasya kuḍavaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13x"><label>6.59.13x</label> haridrāṃ madhukaṃ mūrvāṃ
            mustakaṃ devadāru ca |
            <caesura/>
             pibed akṣasamāṃ kalkāṃ payasā mūtrapīḍitaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xi"><label>6.59.13xi</label> triphalāṃ śūkṣmapiṣṭaṃ vā
            kalkaṃ badarasammitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             vāriṇā lavaṇīkṛtya piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xii"><label>6.59.13xii</label> drākṣārasasya kuḍavaṃ piben
            mūtrarujāharaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nidigdhikāyāḥ svarasaṃ pūtaṃ kuḍavasammitaṃ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xiii"><label>6.59.13xiii</label> mūtradoṣaharam pītvā naraḥ
            sampadyate sukhī ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xiv"><label>6.59.13xiv</label> prapīḍyāmalakānām vā rasaṃ
            kuḍavasammitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pītvāgadībhavej jantur mūtradoṣeṇa pīḍitaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xv"><label>6.59.13xv</label> mūtradoṣe pibed vāpi
            hiṃgvelāpānasaṃyutā |
            <caesura/>
             pānālābhe hitam vāpi svetataṇḍudhāvanaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xvi"><label>6.59.13xvi</label> elāhiṃguyutaṃ kṣīraṃ
            sarpirmiśram piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣo viśudhyarthaṃ śukradoṣaharañ ca tat |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xvii"><label>6.59.13xvii</label> palāśakṣāram āhṛtya
            saptakṛtvāpariśrutaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayet tailasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ mūtradoṣeṇa pīḍitaṃ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xviii"><label>6.59.13xviii</label> adhyardhaprasṛtaṃ vāpi
            tathā sa labhate sukhaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭalīkṣāram āhṛtya palāśakṣāravac ca taṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xix"><label>6.59.13xix</label> vilvasiṃhīyavanāḍaṃ palāśaḥ
            pāribhadrakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             eṣāṃ kṣāram parisrāvya surayā saha saṃsṛjet ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xx"><label>6.59.13xx</label> tatra kalkān imāṃ dadyād
            badarāsthisamanvitāṃ ||
            <caesura/>
             varāṃgamūṣakāṇy elā ślakṣṇaṃ dṛśadi pīṣayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xxi"><label>6.59.13xxi</label> ekatraitat samāloḍya pibec
            charkarayā saha |
            <caesura/>
             eteṣv eva pacet sarpis taṃ lihen madhunā saha |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xxii"><label>6.59.13xxii</label> saguḍakṣārasaṃyuktaṃ
            mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate ||
            <caesura/>
             etat sarvaṃ prayoktavyaṃ mūtrāghāte vijānatā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.14"><label>6.59.14</label> mūtradoṣeṣu kṛcchreṣu tena
            sampadyate gadaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.15"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.16"><label>6.59.16</label> aśmarīśarkarāhetoḥ pūrvam uktaṃ
            cikitsitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             prasamīkṣya yathānyāyaṃ bhiṣak tān api yojayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.17"><label>6.59.17</label> śvadaṃṣṭrāditaṭekuñci hapuṣāṃ
            kaṇṭakārikāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             kālāṃ śatāvarīṃ rāsnāṃ varuṇaṃ sirivālikāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.18"><label>6.59.18</label> vidārigandhādi saṃhṛtya tābhiḥ sa
            tṛvṛtāṃ pibet ||
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā tat peyaṃ tena vāpy anuvāsanaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.19"><label>6.59.19</label> dadyād uttarabastiñ ca
            vātakṛcchropaśāntaye ||
            <caesura/>
             svadaṃṣṭrāsvarase tailaṃ saguḍakṣīranāgaraṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.20"><label>6.59.20</label> paktvā samyak pibet tac ca dadyād
            anilaruggharaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             utpalaṃ tṛṇakākolīnyagrodhādīgaṇe kṛtaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.21"><label>6.59.21</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ pittakṛcchraṃ nāśayet
            kṣīram eva vā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.22"><label>6.59.22</label> ebhir eva kṛtaṃ snehaṃ trividheṣv
            eva bastiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ virecanaṃ cekṣukṣīradrākṣārasair yutaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.23"><label>6.59.23</label> rasaṃ mauṣakamustādi varuṇādau ca
            saṃbhṛtaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ tathā yavāgvādi kaphāghāte praśasyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.24"><label>6.59.24</label> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ kuryād etām eva
            ca sarvaje |
            <caesura/>
             phalguvṛścikadarbhāśmasāracūrṇṇaṃ ca vāriṇā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.25"><label>6.59.25</label> surekṣurasadarbhāmbupītaṃ
            kṛcchrarujāpahaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tathābhighātaje kuryāt sadyo vraṇacikitsitaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.26"><label>6.59.26</label> mūtrakṛcchre sadā cāsya kāryā vā
            vātikī kriyā ||
            <caesura/>
             svedāvagāhāvabhyaṃgaḥ basticūrṇṇakriyās tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.27"><label>6.59.27</label> sakṛjje vā tathānyau tu muddhiṣṭau
            kriyāvidhīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.1"><label>6.60.1</label> athāto mānuṣapratiṣedhaṃ vyāsyāmaḥ
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.2"><label>6.60.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
            śruṇu vatsa suśruta || <anchor n="SS.6.60.2-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.60.2" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Notes">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.60.2-n1"> One of the only two places in the Nepalese
                version where this phrase appears. The other is Suśrutasaṃhitā 5.1.2. At
                that location, a scribe of witness H added the marginal phrase
                  <foreign>atha khalu vatsasuśrutaḥ</foreign>.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.3"><label>6.60.3</label> niśācarebhyo rakṣyas tu nityam eva
            kṣatāturaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             iti yat prāgabhihitaṃ vistarat tasya vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.4"><label>6.60.4</label> grahāṇyaṃ
            gativijñānamanavasthāsahiṣṇutā |
            <caesura/>
             kriyā ś cāmānuṣī yasmiṃ sagrahaḥ parikīrttita<del>ā</del>ḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.5"><label>6.60.5</label> aśucibhinnamayādakṣata taṃ |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsyurhiṃsāvihārārthaṃ satkārārtham athāpi vā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.6"><label>6.60.6</label> asaṃkhyeyāṃ grahāṇyas ttu
            grahādhipatayas tu ye ||
            <caesura/>
             vyañjānte vividhākārā bhidyante te tathāṣṭadhā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.7"><label>6.60.7</label> devās ca devārigaṇyas tathaiva
            gandharvayakṣāḥ pitaro bhujaṅgāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rakṣāṃsi yā cāpi piśācahātireṣoṣṭako devagaṇyai grahaukhyaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.8"><label>6.60.8</label> saṃtuṣṭaḥ sucira vina
            ṣṭagandhamālyau nistandrīr avitathasaṃskṛtābhilāpī |
            <caesura/>
             tejasvī sthitanayano varapradātā brahmaṇyau bhavati ca rudradevajuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.9"><label>6.60.9</label> saṃsvedīṃ dvijagurudevadoṣavaktā
            jihmākṣo vigatabhayo vimārgadṛṣṭiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃtuṣṭo bhavati na cānnapānahātairdraṣṭātmā bhavati ca devaśatrujuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.10"><label>6.60.10</label> hṛṣṭātmā pulinavanāntaropasevī
            svācāraḥ parigatagandhamālyapaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nṛttādyaiḥ prahasati cāru cālpaśabdaṃ gandharvagrahaparipīḍito manuṣyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.11"><label>6.60.11</label> tāmrākṣaḥ
            priyatanuraktavastradhārī gambhīro drutagatiralpavāk sahiṣṇuḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             tejasvī vadati ca kim dadāmi kasmai yo yakṣagrahaparipīḍito manuṣyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.12"><label>6.60.12</label> pretānāṃ nipatati saṃstareṣu
            piṇḍāṃ śāntātmā jalam api cāpasavyahastaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             māṃsepsustilakṛtapāyasābhikāmastadbhakṣo bhavati pitṛgrahābhijuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.13"><label>6.60.13</label> yastūrvyā prasarati sarpavat
            kadācit sṛkvaṇyau vilihati jihvayā tathaiva ||
            <caesura/>
             krordhārttoguḍaṃmadhudugdhapāyasepsurvijñeyo bhavati bhujaṅgamagra hārttaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.14"><label>6.60.14</label>
            māṃsāsṛgvividhasurāvikāralipsurnirlajjo bhṛśamatiniṣṭhuro tiśūraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             krodhārtto vipulabalo niśāvihārī | śaucadviḍ bhavati sa rakṣasā gṛhītaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.15"><label>6.60.15</label> udhdhastaḥ kṛśaparuṣaś cirapralāpī
            durgandho bhṛśamaśucistathātilolaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bahvāśī vijanahimāṃburātrisevī vyācaṣṭaṃ bhramati rudan piśācajuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.16"><label>6.60.16</label> sthūlākṣo drutagamanaḥ saphenalehī
            niṣceṣṭaḥ patati ca vepatethayāti |
            <caesura/>
             yaś cādridviradanagādivicyutaḥ saṃ saṃhṛṣṭo bhavati sahagrahābhijuṣṭaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.17"><label>6.60.17</label> devagrahāḥ paurṇṇāmāsyāmāsurāḥ
            sandhyayor api |
            <caesura/>
             gandhayāḥ prāyaśoṣṭamyāṃ yakṣāś ca pratipatha | </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.18"><label>6.60.18</label> kṛṣṇakṣaye ca pitaraḥ paṇcamyām
            api coragāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rakṣāṃsi rātrau paiśācāś carturdaśyāṃ viśaṃti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.19"><label>6.60.19</label> darpaṇyadīn yathā cchāyā śītoṣṇaṃ
            prāṇino yathā |
            <caesura/>
             mayo bhāskarārcīṃṣi tathā dehaṃ ca dehadhṛk |
            <caesura/>
             viśanti na ca dṛśyante grahāstadvaccharīriṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.20"><label>6.60.20</label> tapāṃsi tīvrāṇi tathaiva dānaṃ
            vratāni dharmo niyataś ca satyaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             grahāstathāṣṭāvapi teṣu nityaṃ vyastāḥ samastāś ca yathāprabhāvaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.21"><label>6.60.21</label> na te manuṣyaiḥ saha saṃviśanti na
            vā manuṣyāṃ kvacidāviśanti |
            <caesura/>
             ye tvāviśantīti vadanti mmūhās te bhūtasargād viṣayādvyapoḍhā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.22"><label>6.60.22</label> teṣāṃ grahāṇāṃ paricārakā ye
            koṭīsahasrāyutapadmasaṃkhyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             asṛgvasāmāṃsabhujaḥ subhīmā niśācarāś cāpi tam āviśanti | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.23"><label>6.60.23</label> niśācarāṇānteṣāṃ hi ye
            devagaṇasaṃrśritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             te tu tat satvasaṃsargāsmaddhruttās tu tadañjanāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.24"><label>6.60.24</label> devagrahā iti khyātāḥ procyante
            śucayas tu te |
            <caesura/>
             devavac ca namasyante pravarttante ca devavat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.25"><label>6.60.25</label> svāmiśīlapriyācārāḥ krama eṣa
            surādiṣu |
            <caesura/>
             nirṛteryā duhitarastāṃsāṃ sa prabhavaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.26"><label>6.60.26</label> sanyāso satpravṛtteṣu vṛttiteṣāṃ
            gaṇaiḥ kṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsāvihārā ye kecid divyam bhāvānapāśritāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.27"><label>6.60.27</label> bhūtānīti kṛtā saṃjña teṣāṃ

            <caesura/>
             grahasañjñāni bhūtāni tasmād budhyaitayo bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.28"><label>6.60.28</label> vidyayā bhūtavaidyatvamatan tvevaṃ
            nirucyate |
            <caesura/>
             te<del>ā</del>ṣāṃ śāntyathamanvicchan vaidyas tu susamāhitaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.29"><label>6.60.29</label> japyaiḥ saniyamaidhīmān ārabheta

            <caesura/>
             raktāni gandhamālyāni bījāni madhusarpiṣī | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.30"><label>6.60.30</label> bhakṣyāś ca sarve sarveṣāṃ sāmānyo

            <caesura/>
             vastrāṇi madyamāṃsāni kṣīrāṇi rudhirāṇi ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.31"><label>6.60.31</label> yāni yeṣāṃ yatheṣṭāni tāni teṣāṃ
            pradāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsanti manujāṃ yeṣu prāyaśo divaseṣu tu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.32"><label>6.60.32</label> devagrahe devagṛhe hutvāgniṃ
            prāpayed baliṃ |<del>|</del>
          </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.33"><label>6.60.33</label>
            kuśasvastikapūpājyacchatrapāyasasaṃyutaṃ |

          <head>[Adhyāya 65]</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.1"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.1</label> athātas tantrayuktyuddeśaṃ
            nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.3"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.3</label> tatra dvātriṃśat
            tantrayuktayo bhavanti |
            <caesura/>
             tad yathā | adhikaraṇam | yogaḥ | padārthaḥ | hetvarthaḥ | uddeśaḥ | nirdeśaḥ
            | upadeśaḥ | apadeśaḥ | pradeśaḥ | atideśaḥ | apavargaḥ | vākyaśeṣaḥ |
            arthāpattiḥ | viparyayaḥ | prasaṅgaḥ | ekāntaḥ | anekāntaḥ | pūrvapakṣaḥ |
            nirṇṇayaḥ | anumatam | vidhānam | anāgatāpekṣaṇam | atikrāntāpekṣaṇaṃ |
            saṃśayaḥ | vyākhyānam | svasaṃjñā | nirvacanam | nidarśanam | niyogaḥ |
            vikalpaḥ | samuccayaḥ | ūhyam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.4"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.4</label> atrāha | āsāṃ yuktīnāṃ kiṃ
            prayojanam | ucyate | vākyayojanam arthayojanañ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.5"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.5</label> ślokau cātra bhavataḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             asadvādiprayuktānāṃ<anchor n="SS.6.65.5-n1"/> śabdānāṃ pratiṣedhanam |
            <caesura/>
             svavākyasiddhir api ca kriyate tantrayuktibhiḥ || </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.5" type="apparatus">
            <list type="note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.65.5-n1">We have adopted the vulgate reading here,
                although it is highly unlikely to be original. In MS H, this pāda appears
                to read <foreign xml:lang="sa">asadaprayuktānāñ ca</foreign>. This is
                unmetrical, the compound is unusual, and there is an unexplained <foreign
                  xml:lang="sa">ca</foreign>. There have been interventions in MS K by a
                second hand, and also there is a hole in the manuscript just at this
                point. The ante correctionem reading of K is unclear but appears to be
                closer to the reading of H than to the vulgate reading. These factors make
                it hard to reconstruct what a plausible and correct older reading might
                have been. For the impact on the meaning of this text, see notes to the
                translation.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.6"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.6</label> vyatyāsoktās tu ye hy arthā
            līnā ye cāpy anirmalāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             leśoktā ye ca kecit syus teṣāñ cāpi prasādhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.7"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.8"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.8</label> tatra yam artham
            adhikṛtyocyate tad adhikaraṇam | yathā rasaṃ doṣaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.9"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.9</label> yena vākyaṃ yujyate sa yogaḥ | yathā
            vyatyāsenoktānāṃ sannikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭānāṃ padārthānām ekīkaraṇam ||<anchor
              n="#SS.6.65.9-n2"/>
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ pibec cāmṛtavallinimba<pc> </pc>haṃsāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             siddhaṃ balābhyāñ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge ||<anchor n="SS.6.65.9-n2"/>

            <caesura/>
             siddhaṃ pibed iti prathamaṃ vaktavye dvitīye pāde siddhaṃ prayuktam |
            <caesura/>
             evan dūrasthānām api padārthānām ekīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ || </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.9" type="apparatus">
            <list type="note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.65.9-n1">The sentence, <foreign>yathā... ekīkaraṇam </foreign>,
                does not appear in the vulgate but an almost identical reading appears in Ḍalhana's
                commentary on this section.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

                Nepalese recension.</note>

              </item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.10"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.10</label> yo 'rtho 'bhihitaḥ sūtre
            pade vā sa padārthaḥ | padasya padayoḥ padānāṃ vā yo 'rthaḥ sa padārthaḥ |
            aparimitāś ca padārthāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yatra tu snehasvedābhyañjaneṣu dvayos trayāṇām vārthānām upapattir dṛśyate
            tatra yo 'rthaḥ pūrvāparayogasiddho bhavati | yathā vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāma ity ukte sandihyate buddhiḥ katamasya vedasyotpattiṃ vakṣyati |
            sāmavedādayaś ca vedāḥ | pūrvāparam upalakṣya vinda vida ity etayoś ca dhātvor
            ekārthaḥ | paścāt padam bhavati āyurvedotpattim ayaṃ vivakṣur iti eṣa
            padārthaḥ |</l>

             yathā mṛtpiṇḍo 'dbhiḥ praklidyate tathā māṣadugdhaprabhṛtibhir vraṇaḥ
            klidyate || </l>

            buddhigamyan tad ūhyam |

            peyam iti | evaṃ caturvidhe vaktavye dvividham abhihitaṃ || atrohyaṃ bhavati
            annapāne viśiṣṭe dvayor grahaṇe caturṇṇām api grahaṇaṃ bhavati ||

            dravasādharmyāt | caturvidhas tv āhāraḥ praviralaḥ | prāyeṇa dvividha eva |
            ato dvitvam prasiddham ity āha bhagavān dhanvantariḥ | </l>

        <div n="66" type="adhyāya">

          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 66: draft edition based on MS K]</head>

          <head>[Adhyāya 66]</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.1"> athāto doṣabhedavikalpam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.3"> aṣṭāṅgāyurvedavidaṃ kāśirājam mahīpatiṃ |<cb/>
            <caesura/>
             cchinnaśāstrārthasandehaṃ sūkṣmāgādhamivodadhiṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.4"> viśvāmitrasutaḥ śrīmāṃ suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||
            <caesura/>
             dviṣaṣṭirdoṣabhedā ye purastātparikīrttitāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.5"> kati tatraikaśo jñeyā viṃśo vāpy athavā triśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasya<cb/> tad vacanaṃ śrutvā saṃśayacchinmahātapāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.6"> prītātmā nṛpaśārdūla suśrutāyāha tattvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trayo doṣā dhātavaś ca pūrīśaṃ mūtram eva ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.7"> dehaṃ sandhārayanty ete hy avyāpannā rasair hitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             puruṣaḥ ṣoḍaṣakalaḥ prāṇāś caikādaśaiva ye | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8ab"> rogāṇāñ ca sahasraṃ yac chata viṃśatir eva ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.9"> vyāsataḥ kīrttitan tadvibhinnā doṣāsu yo guṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dviṣaṣṭidhā bhavanty ete bhūyiṣṭham iti niścayaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.10"> traya eva pṛthag doṣāḥ dviśo nava samādhikāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trayodaśādhikaikadvihīnamadhyordhvalakṣaṇaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.11"> tribhir pañcāśad etan tu sahaivaṃ kṣayam āgataiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hīnamadhyādhikādvekakṣīṇavṛddhās tathāpare </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.12"> dvādaśaiva samākhyātā rogayonir dviṣaṣṭidhā |
            <caesura/>
             miśrā dhātumalairaiva yānty asaṃkhyeyatām api | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.13"> tasmāt prasaṃgaṃ saṃyamya doṣabhedavikalpanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rogaṃ viditvopacared rasabhedair yathe ritaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14"> bhiṣak karttātha karaṇaṃ rasā doṣāś ca kāraṇaṃ ||
            <caesura/>
             kāryam ārogyam evaikam anārogyam athāpi vā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14a"> taśmāt sādhu viditvetāṃ rasadoṣavikalpaṇāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14b"> bhiṣajabheṣajaṃ kāryaṃ prāṇyaṃ hanyan yathā kṛtāṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.15"> adhyāyānāñ ca tuḥ ṣaṣṭyā grathitārthapadakramaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             etad eva viśeṣeṇa tantram uttaram ṛddhimat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16"> spagūḍhārthagambhīram agādhaṃ mandacetasāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             yathākramaṃ yathāpraśnaṃ yathā tatvaṃ yathā vidhiṃ | </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16a">yathā pratijñañ ca mayā bhavatāṃ parikīrttitaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17" met="upajāti"> sahottaran tv etad adhītya tantraṃ
            svāyaṃbhuvaṃ taṃ vidhi<pc> </pc>kīrttitena |
            <caesura/>
             na hīyate rthāṃ manaso bhyupetād evaṃ vaco brāhmyam atīva satyam iti || ❈
            ||</l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17i">mūtradoṣo mūtrāghāto yonyamānūṣa eva ca ||
            <caesura/>
             apasmāronmādakañ caiva rasabhedas tathaiva ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17ii"> svastharakṣāvidhāṇañ ca tantrayuktiś ca doṣabhit |
            <caesura/>
             ity ebhir darśakaṃ proktaṃ punaḥ kāyacikitsite || ❈ ||</l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon1">samāptañ cedaṃ sahottaratantram ity ato nighaṇṭur
            bhaviṣyati || ❈ || </l>

        </div>

        <div type="colophon">

          <head>[<foreign xml:lang="en">Colophon</foreign>]</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon2" met="Sragdharā"> rājye śrīmānadeve pṛthusitayaśasi
            prodyadinduprakāśe
            <caesura/>
             kāle puṇyārjjanasya sakalajanamanohlādiramye vasante
            <caesura/>
             varṣe caikottare 'smiṃs tritayaśatagate mādhave māsi śukle
            <caesura/>
             saptamyāṃ puṣya ṛkṣe daśaśatakiraṇe vāsare siddhayoge </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon3" met="Sragdharā">
            utpattyādyambuvelākulavividharujagrāhajuṣṭātiraudre
            <caesura/>
             saṃsāre sāgare 'smiñ jagad idam akhilaṃ glāninam sampravīkṣya
            <caesura/>
             tasmāc chrīharṣacandro niratiśayaghṛṇābhāvito moktukāmaḥ
            <caesura/>
             prītyā caigaṃ <sic>prākhilat</sic> suśrutākhyam </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.66.colophon3" type="apparatus">
            <list type="notes">
              <item>It is hard to understand how a word ending in <foreign>-gaṃ</foreign>,
                or any accusative, could precede <foreign>prākhilat</foreign> or even
                  <foreign>pra akhilan</foreign>. Some readers have emended <foreign
                  xml:lang="sa">prākhilat</foreign> to <foreign xml:lang="sa"
                  >prālikhat</foreign>, a rare verb, but one that at least governs the
                accusative. We do not see metathesis elsewhere in this scribe's work,
                which is generally very accurate, so we consider the emendation unlikely.
                With so many words missing from this passage, we consider that emendation
                is not useful.</item>

              <item>We read <foreign>-harṣacandro</foreign> which could be the name of the
                scribe. But the following <foreign>nnirati-</foreign> is hard to construe.
                If we read the ablative <foreign>-harṣacandrān</foreign>, it solve the
                problem of <foreign>-nn-</foreign> but is also hard to construe.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon4"> śrīgaṇadevadevakuladūnī gvalakanivāsino
            vaidyavasuvarmaṇaḥ pustakam idaṃ paṭhitvārtham avagamya sarvasattvānām
            upadeśaṃ vidhātuṃ pratipāditam | atas tad ādhikrayābhyāṃ tad gotrajena kenacin
            na kañcid dātavyam | yadā nopakriyate tadāsmān eva pratyarpaṇīyam iti || </l>

        </div>

      </div>
    </body>
  </text>
